[the `unitlessKeys` object shouldn't be emptied (see the `name in unitless` check), as is the case in 4.45.3 and earlier.
`styled-components` uses this to determine wether to add `px` units to CSS like `flex: 1`.](https://github.com/styled-components/styled-components/blob/d0b73acd931daef9eebb97e34fe4552ffc57d63e/packages/styled-components/src/utils/addUnitIfNeeded.ts#L10-L12)

### Actual Behaviour

[It removes all properties and this breaks projects that use `styled-components` with     60	        '!==': (left, right) => left !== right,
    61	        '%': (left: any, right: any) => left % right,
    62	        '&': (left: any, right: any) => left & right,

    64	        // At the moment, "**" will be transpiled to Math.pow

    94	        deoptimizeCache(): void {

    96	        }
    97	
    98	        getLiteralValueAtPath(
    99	                path: ObjectPath,
   100	                recursionTracker: EntityPathTracker,
   101	                origin: DeoptimizableEntity
   102	        ): LiteralValueOrUnknown {
   103	                if (path.length > 0) return UnknownValue;
   104	                const leftValue = this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
   105	                if (typeof leftValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
   106	
   107	                // Optimize `'export' in namespace`
   108	                if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
   109	                        return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
   110	                }
   111	
   112	                const rightValue = this.right.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
   113	                if (typeof rightValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
   114	
   115	                const operatorFunction = binaryOperators[this.operator];
   116	                if (!operatorFunction) return UnknownValue;
   117	
   118	                return operatorFunction(leftValue, rightValue);
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        getRenderedLiteralValue() {
   122	                // Only optimize `'export' in ns`
   123	                if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
   124	
   125	                if (this.renderedLiteralValue !== UNASSIGNED) return this.renderedLiteralValue;
   126	                return (this.renderedLiteralValue = getRenderedLiteralValue(
   127	                        this.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this)
   128	                ));
   129	        }
   130

   138	                        return true;
   139	                }
   140	                return super.hasEffects(context);
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        hasEffectsOnInteractionAtPath(path: ObjectPath, { type }: NodeInteraction): boolean {

   145	        }

   150	                _options?: InclusionOptions
   151	        ) {

   155	                }

    import unitless from '"'"'@emotion/unitless'"'"';

    export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
      if (typeof value === '"'"'number'"'"' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless)) {
        return `${value}px`;
      }
      return String(value).trim();
    }
    """
).strip()

# A simplified stand-in for @emotion/unitless
UNITLESS = textwrap.dedent(
    """
    const unitlessKeys = {
      flex: 1,
      opacity: 1,
      zIndex: 1
    };

    export default unitlessKeys;
    """
).strip()


def run_rollup(versioned_rollup_js):
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
        main = os.path.join(td, '"'"'main.js'"'"')
        unitless = os.path.join(td, '"'"'unitless.js'"'"')
        with open(main, '"'"'w'"'"') as f:
            f.write(ENTRY)
        with open(unitless, '"'"'w'"'"') as f:
            f.write(UNITLESS)

        # use the repository rollup to bundle
        cmd = [
            '"'"'node'"'"',
            '"'"'-e'"'"',
            textwrap.dedent(
                f"""
                const path = require('"'"'path'"'"');
                const rollup = require({json.dumps(versioned_rollup_js)});
                (async () => {{
                  const bundle = await rollup.rollup({{
                    input: {json.dumps(main)},
                    external: ['"'"'@emotion/unitless'"'"'],
                    plugins: [{{
                      name: '"'"'alias-unitless'"'"',
                      resolveId(source) {{
                        if (source === '"'"'@emotion/unitless'"'"') return {json.dumps(unitless)};
                        return null;
                      }}
                    }}]
                  }});
                  const out = await bundle.generate({{format: '"'"'esm'"'"', treeshake: true}});
                  console.log(out.output[0].code);
                }})().catch(e => {{ console.error(e); process.exit(1); }});
                """
            ).strip()
        ]
        res = subprocess.check_output(cmd, cwd=REPO, text=True)
        return res


if __name__ == '"'"'__main__'"'"':
    code = run_rollup('"'"'./dist/rollup.js'"'"')
    # The output should still contain the properties from unitlessKeys object
    # (i.e. not be replaced with an empty object literal).
    print(code)
    if '"'"'flex'"'"' not in code or '"'"'opacity'"'"' not in code:
        raise SystemExit('"'"'Repro failed: unitlessKeys properties were removed'"'"')
    print('"'"'OK: unitlessKeys preserved'"'"')
'

const path = require('path');
const rollup = require('./dist/rollup.js');

(async () => {
  const tmp = require('os').tmpdir();
  const fs = require('fs');
  const dir = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(tmp, 'rollup-in-repro-'));
  const main = path.join(dir, 'main.js');
  const unitless = path.join(dir, 'unitless.js');

  fs.writeFileSync(
    main,
    `import unitless from '@emotion/unitless';

export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless)) {
    return String(value) + 'px';
  }
  return String(value).trim();
}
`
  );

  fs.writeFileSync(
    unitless,
    `const unitlessKeys = { flex: 1, opacity: 1, zIndex: 1 };
export default unitlessKeys;
`
  );

  const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
    input: main,
    plugins: [
      {
        name: 'alias-unitless',
        resolveId(source) {
          if (source === '@emotion/unitless') return unitless;
          return null;
        }
      }
    ]
  });

  const out = await bundle.generate({ format: 'esm' });
  console.log(out.output[0].code);
})();

const unitlessKeys = { };

function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys)) {
    return String(value) + 'px';
  }
  return String(value).trim();
}

export { addUnitIfNeeded as default };

class BinaryExpression extends NodeBase {
    constructor() {
        super(...arguments);
        this.renderedLiteralValue = UNASSIGNED$1;
    }
    deoptimizeCache() {
        this.renderedLiteralValue = UnknownValue;
    }
    getLiteralValueAtPath(path, recursionTracker, origin) {
        if (path.length > 0)
            return UnknownValue;
        const leftValue = this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
        if (typeof leftValue === 'symbol')
            return UnknownValue;
        // Optimize `'export' in namespace`
        if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
            return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
        }
        const rightValue = this.right.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
        if (typeof rightValue === 'symbol')
            return UnknownValue;
        const operatorFunction = binaryOperators[this.operator];
        if (!operatorFunction)
            return UnknownValue;
        return operatorFunction(leftValue, rightValue);
    }
    getRenderedLiteralValue() {
        // Only optimize `'export' in ns`
        if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace)
            return UnknownValue;
        if (this.renderedLiteralValue !== UNASSIGNED$1)
            return this.renderedLiteralValue;
        return (this.renderedLiteralValue = getRenderedLiteralValue(this.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this)));
    }

        // support some implicit type coercion runtime errors

            this.parent instanceof ExpressionStatement &&
            this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this) === '') {
            return true;
        }
        return super.hasEffects(context);
    }
    hasEffectsOnInteractionAtPath(path, { type }) {
        return type !== INTERACTION_ACCESSED || path.length > 1;
    }

        this.included = true;
        if (typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
            super.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively, _options);
        }

        this.included = true;

            this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
        }
    }
    removeAnnotations(code) {

    }

OBSERVATION:

const unitlessKeys = { };

function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys)) {
    return String(value) + 'px';
  }
  return String(value).trim();
}

export { addUnitIfNeeded as default };

        //
        // Do NOT try to evaluate `in` for plain objects, even if the RHS is a
        // compile-time-known object literal. The `in` operator observes the full
        // prototype chain and can trigger Proxy traps, so treating it as a pure
        // operation can lead to incorrect tree-shaking (e.g. removing properties
        // from objects that are used via `name in obj`, as in styled-components).
        if (this.operator === 'in') {
            if (this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
                return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
            }
            return UnknownValue;
        }
        const rightValue = this.right.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
        if (typeof rightValue === 'symbol')
            return UnknownValue;
        const operatorFunction = binaryOperators[this.operator];
        if (!operatorFunction)
            return UnknownValue;
        return operatorFunction(leftValue, rightValue);
    }
    getRenderedLiteralValue() {
        // Only optimize "'export' in namespace" checks.
        // For all other cases, we must not fold the expression as it may observe
        // prototype state or trigger Proxy traps.
        if (this.operator !== 'in' || !(this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable)) {
            return UnknownValue;

            return this.renderedLiteralValue;

const path = require('path');
const rollup = require('./dist/rollup.js');
const fs = require('fs');
const os = require('os');

(async () => {
  const dir = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'rollup-in-repro-'));
  const main = path.join(dir, 'main.js');
  const unitless = path.join(dir, 'unitless.js');

  fs.writeFileSync(
    main,
    `import unitless from '@emotion/unitless';

export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless)) {
    return String(value) + 'px';
  }
  return String(value).trim();
}
`
  );

  fs.writeFileSync(
    unitless,
    `const unitlessKeys = { flex: 1, opacity: 1, zIndex: 1 };
export default unitlessKeys;
`
  );

  const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
    input: main,
    treeshake: true,
    plugins: [
      {
        name: 'alias-unitless',
        resolveId(source) {
          if (source === '@emotion/unitless') return unitless;
          return null;
        }
      }
    ]
  });

  const out = await bundle.generate({ format: 'esm' });
  console.log(out.output[0].code);
})();

const unitlessKeys = { };

function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys)) {
    return String(value) + 'px';
  }
  return String(value).trim();
}

const path = require('path');
const rollup = require('./dist/rollup.js');
const fs = require('fs');
const os = require('os');

(async () => {
  const dir = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'rollup-in-repro-'));
  const main = path.join(dir, 'main.js');
  const unitless = path.join(dir, 'unitless.js');

  fs.writeFileSync(
    main,
    `import unitless from '@emotion/unitless';

export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless)) {
    return String(value) + 'px';
  }
  return String(value).trim();
}
`
  );

  fs.writeFileSync(
    unitless,
    `const unitlessKeys = { flex: 1, opacity: 1, zIndex: 1 };
export default unitlessKeys;
`
  );

  const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
    input: main,
    plugins: [
      {
        name: 'alias-unitless',
        resolveId(source) {
          if (source === '@emotion/unitless') return unitless;
          return null;
        }
      }
    ]
  });

  const out = await bundle.generate({ format: 'esm' });
  console.log(out.output[0].code);
})();

@@ -0,0 +1,80 @@
+import json, os, subprocess, textwrap, tempfile
+
+REPO = '/testbed'
+
+# Repro based on the PR description: an object literal used as RHS for `in`
+# should not be optimized away/emptied by Rollup tree-shaking.
+ENTRY = textwrap.dedent(
+    """
+    import unitless from '@emotion/unitless';
+
+    export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
+      if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless)) {
+        return `${value}px`;
+      }
+      return String(value).trim();
+    }
+    """
+).strip()
+
+# A simplified stand-in for @emotion/unitless
+UNITLESS = textwrap.dedent(
+    """
+    const unitlessKeys = {
+      flex: 1,
+      opacity: 1,
+      zIndex: 1
+    };
+
+    export default unitlessKeys;
+    """
+).strip()
+
+
+def run_rollup(versioned_rollup_js):
+    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
+        main = os.path.join(td, 'main.js')
+        unitless = os.path.join(td, 'unitless.js')
+        with open(main, 'w') as f:
+            f.write(ENTRY)
+        with open(unitless, 'w') as f:
+            f.write(UNITLESS)
+
+        # use the repository rollup to bundle
+        cmd = [
+            'node',
+            '-e',
+            textwrap.dedent(
+                f"""
+                const path = require('path');
+                const rollup = require({json.dumps(versioned_rollup_js)});
+                (async () => {{
+                  const bundle = await rollup.rollup({{
+                    input: {json.dumps(main)},
+                    external: ['@emotion/unitless'],
+                    plugins: [{{
+                      name: 'alias-unitless',
+                      resolveId(source) {{
+                        if (source === '@emotion/unitless') return {json.dumps(unitless)};
+                        return null;
+                      }}
+                    }}]
+                  }});
+                  const out = await bundle.generate({{format: 'esm'}});
+                  console.log(out.output[0].code);
+                }})().catch(e => {{ console.error(e); process.exit(1); }});
+                """
+            ).strip()
+        ]
+        res = subprocess.check_output(cmd, cwd=REPO, text=True)
+        return res
+
+
+if __name__ == '__main__':
+    code = run_rollup('./dist/rollup.js')
+    # The output should still contain the properties from unitlessKeys object
+    # (i.e. not be replaced with an empty object literal).
+    print(code)
+    if 'flex' not in code or 'opacity' not in code:
+        raise SystemExit('Repro failed: unitlessKeys properties were removed')
+    print('OK: unitlessKeys preserved')

@@ -104,9 +104,18 @@ export default class BinaryExpression extends NodeBase implements DeoptimizableE
 		const leftValue = this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
 		if (typeof leftValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
 
-		// Optimize `'export' in namespace`
-		if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
-			return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
+		// We can only safely optimize "'<name>' in <namespace>" checks.
+		//
+		// Do NOT try to evaluate `in` for plain objects, even if the RHS is a
+		// compile-time-known object literal. The `in` operator observes the full
+		// prototype chain and can trigger Proxy traps, so treating it as a pure
+		// operation can lead to incorrect tree-shaking (e.g. removing properties
+		// from objects that are used via `name in obj`, as in styled-components).
+		if (this.operator === 'in') {
+			if (this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
+				return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
+			}
+			return UnknownValue;
 		}
 
 		const rightValue = this.right.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
@@ -119,8 +128,12 @@ export default class BinaryExpression extends NodeBase implements DeoptimizableE
 	}
 
 	getRenderedLiteralValue() {
-		// Only optimize `'export' in ns`
-		if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
+		// Only optimize "'export' in namespace" checks.
+		// For all other cases, we must not fold the expression as it may observe
+		// prototype state or trigger Proxy traps.
+		if (this.operator !== 'in' || !(this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable)) {
+			return UnknownValue;
+		}
 
 		if (this.renderedLiteralValue !== UNASSIGNED) return this.renderedLiteralValue;
 		return (this.renderedLiteralValue = getRenderedLiteralValue(

+			// If we can fold the `in` check, the RHS is a namespace and we include it.
+			// Otherwise, we must still include the RHS expression as its shape
+			// influences runtime behaviour and may depend on treeshaken properties.
 			this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
 		}
